<rating>5< /rating>< review>
Working with this company was great!  The sales representative showed up promptly as scheduled and quickly did the necessary measurements for the fence as we discussed details and warranty.  They were very accommodating and didn't try to nickle and dime for every little thing.  The quote was actually the cheapest out of all the quotes I received and their service was amazing.

When they found a post that wasn't quite aligned to their liking, they took the time to break up the concrete, adjust the post and repour concrete. < text>
Super chill atmosphere. Lots of space to sit or even lounge in couches. I can't speak on behalf of the food, but the drinks are absolutely incredible! They definitely have their own version of cocktails that I've never had before.

I was originally going to give four stars but on the last drink the bartender actually came over to our table and lit it on fire and did an entire show, it was so awesome! It was called the forbidden. He said he doesn't always do it tableside, so don't expect it, but when he has time he does.

We would recommend this. We will be back for happy hour.< /text>

<Time>1548295549331< /Time>< review>
Darkly wood panelled place, dine in the pseudo "old" style. Overstuffed stools, a couch or two and a secondary bar level stooped area make for abundant seating. Service was uneven, as it took the staff over 10 minutes to notice that we were there (not many of them were out) but once we were noticed, a number of servers and associated workers appeared, as if they were all occupied elsewhere and just got let out; it was odd. The service, once the servers were "out", was prompt and professional. Drinks are not cheap but I had the feeling they are trying to represent themselves as an "established" place but the feel was more if an "upscaley" place; we're popular and you're fortunate to be eating our fine food. The food was quite good. The drinks were quite tasty (they know what they're doing) but I wouldn't go there for drinks (too little for what is charged) unless I pulled in 100k yearly, imho.  4.5 STARS<//review>

<rating>5<//rating><Review>White Horse is a really great place to visit for delicious New Orleans Cajun. The food and drinks are very well priced for the outstanding quality you get, and the servers and bartenders are extremely knowledgeable as well. Feel safe when visiting, everything is being done with the COVID best practice requirements. Great happy hour offerings as well, especially for those that like 'Old Fashioneds'. I really liked and appreciated the old school music and old fashioned dim bar surroundings, it really was refreshing. The dark wood and red upholstery The exterior design is very tasteful and catches your attention when passing by. The set up works great for those looking for a group setting or even just for couples. I found the brunch menu to be especially enticing, I'm going to need to come back a couple of times to try out all the things that looked promising. The parking structure is right next door for maximum convenience. This place is truly a hidden gem amongst all the other great places in Pasadena. I'm also looking forward to checking out their sister location, Craft Hill, which I've heard great things about. Brandon was an amazing team member and recommended the fried chicken sandwich, which was fantastic. He knew all the items on the menu almost from memory and went above and beyond to walk me through everything. I'm glad I went with his recommendations. He also told me some cool things to do in the area and South Pasadena, so I have those on my list as well. They don't skip on the portions either, you'll definitely satisfy your appetite and probably have some leftovers as well. I can't think of much they can do to improve things, everything was so great! I plan on visiting again sooner rather than later.< /Review>< Pics>

I like to cook. I do. I really really do. So I already know when I go out to eat that I can prepare the meal I‚Äôm going to eat just as well as the restaurant for a fraction of the price. Therefore service, ambiance, and cleanliness are of the upmost importance to me.

<username>James Wan< /username><date>1583312770688</date><rating>2<//rating><review>A packed dining room and bar put this place quite in the limelight as you enter on a weekend evening. Unfortunately, there were far too many misses to honestly click on an extra star for the rating.

The bar seriously needs to pay attention to customers. Waiting for my party and waiting at the bar, and trying to get a drink was an impossible 5 minutes. They were treating me like I just came out of an AA meeting.

The menu seems to hit most of the notes for a hungry patron. At first glance, you can see it is well designed. Something for everyone wraps the context of each category. Fine Wagyu meats, a great burger, your standard salmon dish, and an attractive Southern Fried Chicken.

Dig deeper and you can find the pretentiousness of certain items. The use of Wagyu in smoked brisket, for example, is quite a redundancy. Why pay for a Wagyu priced cut that is supposed to be slow-smoked/cooked?

The Jumbalaya Rissoto is in fact not "risotto," and made with orzo pasta. Granted it is stated in the description as orzo, the title is completely misleading. If a person was gluten intolerant this would be a horrific experience. This dish is totally not worthy of the $26 price tag for a pasta dish.

The service felt like the servers were really working hard. I overheard a waiter mumbling about covering 8 large tables. I commend the service timing for everyone at the table.

The drinks here are very good. The bar certainly displays some craft behind their creations. I would return for their happy hour, and possibly a revisit for a sample of other items.

I do miss Cheval Blanc that once took this location to new heights in french cuisine.< /review>< pictures>

I've only come here for the bar and drinks, never had the food. The drinks are all great, well thought out, and delicious. I came here last night for my birthday. First I gotta say the food deserves 5 stars. The food was fresh and delicious. I'm knocking off 3 stars because of our interaction with the Manager Cameron. My wife reserved a room for my birthday party and out of nowhere the waitress let us know we had 10 minutes to clear the room (decorations, etc.) because another party was going to sit there. They  didn't even have another table to transition us to. The waitress was pretty much like, "I guess you can sit at one of the other tables." Odd thing is, once we moved to the outside area we never saw anyone move into where we sitting. So why have us move out? My wife complained to the Manager Cameron about this and he preceded to argue back with my wife for about 30 minutes. He explained to my wife that the party that was going to move into our section decided to stay at the bar area afterall. We will  never be back to this restaurant again, which is a shame because like I said, the food was delicious. The way Cameron handled this situation was poor. Somebody needs to train this guy on how to provide good customer service. There is no excuse for him to try to win an argument with a paying customer (we spent over $900). Josh was proud of his cooking style learned from her Japanese granma.

We came to White Horse Lounge in Pasadena to celebrate a friend's birthday.
Love the beautiful bar area. It‚Äôs got that classic American bar vibe.
Since we have a large party, we were seated in the private room in the back.
Very simple one page menu. They have quite a few small bites that are great with drinks.

Market Hummus | $10
House Lavash, EVOO, Fresh Garnish
We ordered a few appetizers to share.
Market Hummus was just ok. It lacked flavor.

Seared Brussel Sprouts | $10
Smoked Tomatoes, Basil, Parmesan
Seared Brussel Sprouts was great. We enjoyed the addition of tomatoes and basil.

Garlic Truffle Fries | $9
Truffle Oil, Parmesan, Gremolata
We love the Garlic Truffle Fries. Thick and crunchy fries seasoned with truffle oil and cheese.

Bone-In New York 22 oz | $45
For steak orders, guests can pick 2 sides and a sauce for the meat.
A friend ordered the huge Bone-In New York, and she almost finished it!
She likes the steak, but didn‚Äôt like the cajun butter sauce.

Ribeye 16 oz | $35
Dr. P and I both ordered the Ribeye.
The steak was cooked perfectly. Very delicious.
For sides, I got the twice baked potato and corn succotash.
I enjoyed both. And the horseradish sauce was great with the steak.

The Black Sea | $25
Squid Ink Tagliolini, Dinapoli Tomato, Calamari, Prawn, Fin√©s Herbes
A few people ordered The Black Sea ‚Äì the squid ink seafood pasta.
Everyone said it was way too salty, and nobody liked it.

I like that we had the private room, and could be as loud as we want.
Service could be better. Our waitress didn‚Äôt check on us often.
We had to go out to find her a few times.
It was a really fun night with friends.<//text>
